25 /**
26  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
27  */
28 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
29                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
30                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
31                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
32                                 val userService: UserService,
33                                 eventService: EventService,
34                                 locationService: LocationService,
35                                 importService: ImportService)
36     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
37     extends AbstractController(cc)
38     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
39     with Util {
40 
41   val log = Logger("api.event")
42 
43   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
44     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
45 
46     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
47 
48     db.run(q.detailed).flatMap(x => x.headOption match {
49       case Some(r) => {
50         if (!r.location.latitude.isDefined || r.location.latitude == Some(0)) {
51           locationService.geocode(r.location).map(l => Ok(Json.toJson(r.copy(location = l))))
52         } else {
53           Future.successful(Ok(Json.toJson(r)))
54         }
55       }
56       case _ => Future.successful(NotFound)
57     })
58   }
59 
60   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
61                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
62     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
63     
64     val q = for {
65       e <- event if e.name like search.map(y => "%"++y++"%").getOrElse("%%").bind
66                  /*if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""*/
67                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
68                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
69                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
70                  if e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp
71     } yield e
72 
73 
74 
75     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
76     returnPaged(s,q,db)
77   }
78 
79   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
80     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
81 
82     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
83 
84     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
85       case Some(e) => {
86         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
87           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
88               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
89           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
90         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
91         returnPaged(s,q,db)
92       }
93       case None => Future(NotFound)
94     }
95   }
96 
97   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
98     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
99 
100     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
101       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
102       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
103       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
104 
105     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
106 
107     returnPaged(s,q,db)
108   }
109 
110   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
111     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
112 
113     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
114 
115     db.run(q).map {
116       case 0 => NotFound
117       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
118     }
119   }
120 
121   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
122     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
123       form => {
124         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
125       },
126       data => {
127         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
128 
129         eventService.insertEvent(data, organizer).map {
130           case Some(ev) => Ok(Json.toJson(ev))
131           case None => BadRequest
132         }
133       })
134   }
135 
136   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
137     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
138       form => {
139         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
140       },
141       data => {
142         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
143 
144         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
145 
146         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
147 
148         val catParents = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
149             case cat =>
150               cat.id match {
151                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).flatMap(_.parent).result
152               }
153           }
154 
155         val catSimple = data.categories.filter(_.id.isDefined).map {
156             case cat =>
157               cat.id match {
158                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
159               }
160           }
161         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(catSimple ++ catParents).map(_.flatten.distinct)
162 
163         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
164 
165         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
166           case (((images,categories),Some(event)),Some(location)) => {
167             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
168                               data.description,
169                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
170                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
171 
172             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
173 
174             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
175               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
176           }
177           case _ => Future.successful(None)
178         }.flatMap {
179           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
180             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
181             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
182             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
183 
184             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
185             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
186             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
187             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
188           }
189           case None => Future.successful(None)
190         }.map {
191           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
192           case None => BadRequest
193         }
194       })
195   }
196 
197   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
198     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
199 
200     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
201       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
202 
203       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
204      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
205   }
206 
207   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
208     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
209 
210     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
211       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
212 
213     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
214       case (Some(e),None) => {
215         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
216         Future.successful(Ok)
217       }
218       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
219       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
220     }
221   }
222 
223   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
224     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
225 
226     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
227       .flatMap {
228       case 1 => {
229         Future.successful(Ok)
230       }
231       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
232     }
233   }
234 
235   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
236     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
237 
238     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
239   }
240 
241   def importFacebookEvent(url: String) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
242     log.debug("Rest request to import event from url")
243 
244     importService.getEvent(url, request.identity)
245       .map(x => x.map(y => Ok(Json.toJson(y))).getOrElse(BadRequest))
246   }
247   
248   def copy(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { case (request,organizer) =>
249     log.debug("Rest request to copy event")
250 
251     db.run(EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id && x.creatorId === organizer.id).detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
252       case Some(ev) => {
253         val locationForm = LocationForm.Data(ev.location.id, ev.location.name, ev.location.country,
254                                              ev.location.city, ev.location.street, ev.location.website,
255                                              ev.location.phone, ev.location.comment, ev.location.link, ev.location.zip)
256         val eventForm = EventForm.Data(ev.name, ev.from, ev.to, ev.categories.map(_.category), locationForm, 
257                                   ev.images.map(x => TaggedImageForm.Data(x.id.get, x.tag)), ev.description, ev.priceMin, ev.priceMax)
258         
259         eventService.insertEvent(eventForm, organizer).map {
260           case Some(event) => Ok(Json.toJson(event))
261           case _ => BadRequest
262         }
263       }
264       case None => Future.successful(BadRequest)
265     }
266   }
